Board Committees The Board has standing Compensation Committee, Nominating and Corporate Governance Committee (" Nominating Committee" ) and Audit and Finance Committee (" Audit Committee "). The Compensation Committee primarily responsible for reviewing the compensation arrangements for the Company\' executive officers, including the Chief Executive Officer, and for administering the Company\' stock option plans. Members the Compensation Committee are Messrs. Campbell, Drexler, Gore and . Levinson. The Nominating Committee assists the Board identifying qualified individuals become directors, determines the composition the Board and its committees, monitors the process assess Board effectiveness and helps develop and implement the Company\' corporate governance guidelines. Members the Nominating Committee are Messrs. Campbell, Drexler, Gore and . Levinson. The Audit Committee primarily responsible for overseeing the services performed the Company\' independent auditors and internal audit department, evaluating the Company\' accounting policies and its system internal controls and reviewing significant financial transactions. Consistent with the Nasdaq audit committee structure and membership requirements, the Audit Committee comprised three members: Messrs. Campbell, York and . Levinson. Because . York\' affiliation with MicroWarehouse, (see Item . Certain Relationships and Related Transactions), deemed "non-independent" director. permitted under the Nasdaq requirements, the Board carefully considered . York\' affiliation with MicroWarehouse well his accounting and financial expertise and determined that the best interest the Company and its shareholders that continue serve member the Audit Committee. Both . Campbell and . Levinson are independent directors. The Audit, Compensation and Nominating Committees operate under written charters adopted the Board. These charters are available the Company\' website www apple com investor. Arrangements with Named Executive Officers Change Control Arrangements\x97Stock Options the event "change control" the Company, all outstanding options under the Company\' stock option plans, except the Director Plan, will, unless otherwise determined the plan administrator, become exercisable full, and will cashed out amount equal the difference between the applicable "change control price" and the exercise price. The Director Plan provides that upon "change control" the Company, all unvested options held non-employee directors will automatically become fully vested and exercisable and will cashed out amount equal the difference between the applicable "change control price" and the exercise price the options. "change control" under these plans generally defined ( ) the acquisition any person % more the combined voting power the Company\' outstanding securities ( ) the occurrence transaction requiring shareholder approval and involving the sale all substantially all the assets the Company the merger the Company with into another corporation. addition, options granted the Named Executive Officers generally provide that the event there "change control," defined the Company\' stock option plans, and connection with following such "change control," their employment terminated without "Cause" they should resign for "Good Reason," those options outstanding that are not yet vested and exercisable the date such "change control" shall become fully vested and exercisable. Generally, "Cause" defined include felony conviction, willful disclosure confidential information willful and continued failure perform his her employment duties. Policy Audit Committee Pre-Approval Audit and Non-Audit Services Performed the Independent Auditors Prior the enactment the Sarbanes-Oxley Act (the " Act "), the Company adopted auditor independence policy that banned its auditors from performing non-financial consulting services, such information technology consulting and internal audit services. This auditor policy also mandates that annual budget for both audit and non-audit services approved the Audit Committee advance, and that the Audit Committee provided with quarterly reporting actual spending. This policy also mandates that auditor engagements for non-audit services may entered into without the express approval the Audit Committee. Board Committees The Board has standing Compensation Committee, Nominating and Corporate Governance Committee (" Nominating Committee" ) and Audit and Finance Committee (" Audit Committee "). The Compensation Committee primarily responsible for reviewing the compensation arrangements for the Company\' executive officers, including the Chief Executive Officer, and for administering the Company\' stock option plans. Members the Compensation Committee are Messrs. Campbell, Drexler, Gore and . Levinson. The Nominating Committee assists the Board identifying qualified individuals become directors, determines the composition the Board and its committees, monitors the process assess Board effectiveness and helps develop and implement the Company\' corporate governance guidelines. Members the Nominating Committee are Messrs. Campbell, Drexler, Gore and . Levinson. The Audit Committee primarily responsible for overseeing the services performed the Company\' independent auditors and internal audit department, evaluating the Company\' accounting policies and its system internal controls and reviewing significant financial transactions. Section ( ) Beneficial Ownership Reporting Compliance Section ( ) the Securities Exchange Act , amended, requires the Company\' officers and directors, and persons who own more than ten percent registered class the Company\' equity securities, file reports securities ownership and changes such ownership with the Securities and Exchange Commission (" SEC "). Officers, directors and greater than ten percent shareholders also are required rules promulgated the SEC furnish the Company with copies all Section ( ) forms they file. Based solely upon review the copies such forms furnished the Company written representations that Forms were required, the Company believes that all Section ( ) filing requirements were met during fiscal year , except that Messrs. Arrangements with Named Executive Officers Change Control Arrangements\x97Stock Options the event "change control" the Company, all outstanding options under the Company\' stock option plans, except the Director Plan, will, unless otherwise determined the plan administrator, become exercisable full, and will cashed out amount equal the difference between the applicable "change control price" and the exercise price. The Director Plan provides that upon "change control" the Company, all unvested options held non-employee directors will automatically become fully vested and exercisable and will cashed out amount equal the difference between the applicable "change control price" and the exercise price the options. "change control" under these plans generally defined ( ) the acquisition any person % more the combined voting power the Company\' outstanding securities ( ) the occurrence transaction requiring shareholder approval and involving the sale all substantially all the assets the Company the merger the Company with into another corporation. addition, options granted the Named Executive Officers generally provide that the event there "change control," defined the Company\' stock option plans, and connection with following such "change control," their employment terminated without "Cause" they should resign for "Good Reason," those options outstanding that are not yet vested and exercisable the date such "change control" shall become fully vested and exercisable. Generally, "Cause" defined include felony conviction, willful disclosure confidential information willful and continued failure perform his her employment duties. "Good Reason" includes resignation employment result substantial diminution position duties, adverse change title reduction annual base salary. Item . Policy Audit Committee Pre-Approval Audit and Non-Audit Services Performed the Independent Auditors Prior the enactment the Sarbanes-Oxley Act (the " Act "), the Company adopted auditor independence policy that banned its auditors from performing non-financial consulting services, such information technology consulting and internal audit services. This auditor policy also mandates that annual budget for both audit and non-audit services approved the Audit Committee advance, and that the Audit Committee provided with quarterly reporting actual spending. This policy also mandates that auditor engagements for non-audit services may entered into without the express approval the Audit Committee.
